Ring of the Dreadnaught
(2) Set:
Your Sweeping Strikes and Death Wish abilities cost 100 less Rage.

(6) Set:

(8) Set:
Your melee critical strikes cause you to shout a rallying cry, increasing the physical damage of your party members' next attack by 30.
